Dimensional multiplier before UV-divergent part of the integrand (with symmetric coefficient), i.e. C_int_lambda: 
4*I*Pi^2*Cutoff^(-2*d - 4*eps + 1)*go^2*nuo*rho*lcs[s, 0, 9]*mom[p, s]
Dimensional multiplier before UV-convergent part of the integrand (with symmetric coefficient), i.e. C_int_B: 
4*I*Pi^2*B^(-2*d - 4*eps + 1)*go^2*nuo^(2*d + 4*eps)*rho*lcs[s, 0, 9]*mom[p, s]
